name:M‚Äça‚Äçr‚Äçk
info:Deluxe Garden View Room
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:3.2
posted:Posted August 15, 2023
msg:Breakfast had a vast selection, but none of it was very good. The sushi would make a Japanese person cry, the sausages and bacon would make an English person cry and you would get a better Chinese breakfast for 10RMB at a local market (baozi and yotiao are from frozen).

The main reason for choosing this hotel over other options was the kids club. Unfortunately it is rubbish. A single member of staff doing some origami with leaves or basic art/craft. Requires adult supervision. Very disappointing by international standards.

Hotel is very grand, but not maintained to the standard you would expect from the brand. Design of the hotel does not lend itself to Haikou's climate, the communal spaces are not aircondionable and so it is uncomfortably hot.

Pool was good, but again needs maintenance. Children especially enjoyed the foam cannon.

Room was spacious, clean and cool. 

Coffee is good.

At the time of writing they offer "good night" as a free gift which is a lavender spray. They also offer a free drink on arrival - which just means help yourself to a drink from the fridge in your room.

Overall I would recommend paying a bit less and going with a newer hotel closer to the city.

msg:The hotel is in a beautiful location on the bay area, west of Haikou and amongst other big hotels. Check-in was seamless and easy, even though I arrived late at night. Morning breakfast was a big buffet with both Chinese and Western options...very good in my opinion. The room was well-appointed with a nice bathtub, TV and a balcony overlooking the sea, great for sunrises in the morning. The pool was fantastic and the bar service very good, as I could get cold beers brought to me next to the pool. Staff were very friendly. The only downside was there was flying ants or insects in the room during the second night and I got badly bitten on the body while I slept. Not sure what it was. Manager investigated the problem and tried his best to resolve it. The hotel offered to refund me money, which I accepted and they apologized and were very sincere and professional in their handling of the situation. Hainan is a tropical climate, so these things happen sometimes.

The hotel service is very considerate, and all kinds of small needs can be responded in time.

All in all, it meets the standards of a five-star luxury hotel. The scenery is beautiful and quiet. Compared with the more popular hotels in Sanya, it is more suitable for families who are lazy and just want to relax.

Perhaps for the big security guard, the cleanliness and orderliness of the entrance of the famous hotel Marriott is far more important than the warmth of the guests.
